<h1 class='title'>
<a href='http://semi-madman.blogspot.com/'>Ramblings of a Semi-Mad Man</a>
</h1>
</div>
<div class='descriptionwrapper'>
<p class='description'><span>Welcome to our Ramblings!!! This little blog is about life.  We are here to entertain, inform and make your life better.  We hope to give you a laugh to start your day, make you think a little and stimulate your senses.  We will be blogging about anything and everything.  Sports, Women, Music, Politics, Relationships, Sex, Movies, Education...If you can think it, we will surely blog about it!  Sit back and enjoy "The Ramblings of a Semi-Mad Man!"</span></p>
</div>
